16.2-inch barrel, collapsible stock, flat-top receiver with detachable carry handle, CAR handguards, flash hider, A2 pistol grip, and 30-round magazine.</font></p> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="2">A tactical .22 rifle like this Colt is ideal for new shooters who are learning handling and operation.
